         <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="China"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a></b>&nbsp;– People's Republic of China<sup id="cite_ref-ChinaTaiwan_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ChinaTaiwan-21">[l]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td> 
         <td style="background:LightCoral;"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Foreign_relations_of_China&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Foreign relations of China (not yet started)">Partially unrecognized</a>. <span style="display:none">B Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a> </span>Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a></span> </td> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">The People's Republic of China (PRC) contains five autonomous regions:<sup id="cite_ref-autonomous_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-autonomous-8">[f]</a></sup> 
          <ul>
           <li><a href="/wiki/Guangxi" title="Guangxi">Guangxi</a></li> 
           <li><a href="/wiki/Inner_Mongolia" title="Inner Mongolia">Inner Mongolia</a></li> 
           <li><a href="/wiki/Ningxia" title="Ningxia">Ningxia</a></li> 
           <li><a href="/wiki/Xinjiang" title="Xinjiang">Xinjiang</a></li> 
           <li><a href="/wiki/Tibet_Autonomous_Region" class="mw-redirect" title="Tibet Autonomous Region">Tibet</a></li>
          </ul> <p>Additionally, it has sovereignty over the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Special_administrative_regions_of_China&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Special administrative regions of China (not yet started)">Special Administrative Regions</a> of: </p> 
          <ul>
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Flag_of_Hong_Kong.svg/23px-Flag_of_Hong_Kong.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Flag_of_Hong_Kong.svg/35px-Flag_of_Hong_Kong.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5b/Flag_of_Hong_Kong.svg/45px-Flag_of_Hong_Kong.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a></li> 
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Flag_of_Macau.svg/23px-Flag_of_Macau.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Flag_of_Macau.svg/35px-Flag_of_Macau.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Flag_of_Macau.svg/45px-Flag_of_Macau.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="341">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a></li>
          </ul> <p>China claims, but does not control <a href="#Taiwan">Taiwan</a>, which is governed by a rival administration (the Republic of China) that claims all of China as its territory.<sup id="cite_ref-TAI2_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TAI2-22">[m]</a></sup> </p><p>China is not recognised by <a href="/w/index.php?title=Foreign_relations_of_China&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Foreign relations of China (not yet started)">19</a> UN member states and the <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Holy See</a>, which, with the exception of Bhutan, recognise Taiwan instead.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">[n]</a></sup> </p><p>China controls part of the territory of <a href="/wiki/Kashmir" title="Kashmir">Kashmir</a>, which is disputed by <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>. </p> </td>
        </tr>

         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Member of the EU.<sup id="cite_ref-EU_3-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EU-3">[c]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Denmark" class="mw-redirect" title="Kingdom of Denmark">Kingdom of Denmark</a> includes 2 self-governing territories: 
          <ul>
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Flag_of_the_Faroe_Islands.svg/21px-Flag_of_the_Faroe_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Flag_of_the_Faroe_Islands.svg/32px-Flag_of_the_Faroe_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Flag_of_the_Faroe_Islands.svg/41px-Flag_of_the_Faroe_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1100" data-file-height="800">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Faroe_Islands" title="Faroe Islands">Faroe Islands</a></li> 
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_Greenland.svg/23px-Flag_of_Greenland.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_Greenland.svg/35px-Flag_of_Greenland.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/09/Flag_of_Greenland.svg/45px-Flag_of_Greenland.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Greenland" title="Greenland">Greenland</a></li>
          </ul> <p>The continental territory of Denmark, the Faroe Islands, and Greenland form the three constituent countries of the Kingdom. The designation "Denmark" can refer either to continental Denmark or to the short name for the entire Kingdom (e.g. in international organizations). The Kingdom of Denmark as a whole is a member of the EU, but EU law does not apply to the Faroe Islands and Greenland.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">[13]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">[14]</a></sup> Also see <a href="/w/index.php?title=Greenland_Treaty&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Greenland Treaty (not yet started)">Greenland Treaty</a>. </p> </td>

         <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Israel"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/21px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png" decoding="async" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/32px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/41px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1100" data-file-height="800">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israel</a></b>&nbsp;– State of Israel </td> 
         <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td> 
         <td style="background:LightCoral;"><a href="/w/index.php?title=International_recognition_of_Israel&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="International recognition of Israel (not yet started)">Partially unrecognized</a> </td> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Israel exerts strong control over the territory claimed by <a href="#Palestine">Palestine</a>. Israel annexed <a href="/w/index.php?title=East_Jerusalem&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="East Jerusalem (not yet started)">East Jerusalem</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">[25]</a></sup> an annexation not recognised by the international community.<sup id="cite_ref-dis_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-dis-48">[26]</a></sup> Israel maintains <a href="/w/index.php?title=West_Bank_Areas_in_the_Oslo_II_Accord&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="West Bank Areas in the Oslo II Accord (not yet started)">varying levels of control</a> over the rest of the <a href="/wiki/West_Bank" title="West Bank">West Bank</a>, and although Israel no longer has a permanent civilian or military presence in the <a href="/wiki/Gaza_Strip" title="Gaza Strip">Gaza Strip</a>, following its <a href="/w/index.php?title=Israel%27s_unilateral_disengagement_plan&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Israel's unilateral disengagement plan (not yet started)">unilateral disengagement</a>, it is still considered by some to be the occupying power under international law. <p><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">[27]</a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">[28]</a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">[29]</a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">[30]</a></sup> <sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">[31]</a></sup> Israel is not recognised as a state by <a href="/w/index.php?title=International_recognition_of_Israel&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="International recognition of Israel (not yet started)">32 UN members</a> (including most Arab states) nor by the <a href="/wiki/Sahrawi_Arab_Democratic_Republic" title="Sahrawi Arab Democratic Republic">SADR</a>. </p> </td>
        </tr>

         <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Netherlands"></span><b><span class="datasortkey" data-sort-value="Netherlands"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span></b>&nbsp;– Kingdom of the Netherlands </td> 
         <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td> 
         <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None </td> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Member of the EU.<sup id="cite_ref-EU_3-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-EU-3">[c]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_the_Netherlands" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands">Kingdom of the Netherlands</a> includes four areas with substantial autonomy: 
          <ul>
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Aruba.svg/23px-Flag_of_Aruba.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Aruba.svg/35px-Flag_of_Aruba.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f6/Flag_of_Aruba.svg/45px-Flag_of_Aruba.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Aruba" title="Aruba">Aruba</a></li> 
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Flag_of_Cura%C3%A7ao.svg/23px-Flag_of_Cura%C3%A7ao.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Flag_of_Cura%C3%A7ao.svg/35px-Flag_of_Cura%C3%A7ao.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b1/Flag_of_Cura%C3%A7ao.svg/45px-Flag_of_Cura%C3%A7ao.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Cura%C3%A7ao" title="Curaçao">Curaçao</a></li> 
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/20/Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Netherlands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a></li> 
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Flag_of_Sint_Maarten.svg/23px-Flag_of_Sint_Maarten.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Flag_of_Sint_Maarten.svg/35px-Flag_of_Sint_Maarten.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d3/Flag_of_Sint_Maarten.svg/45px-Flag_of_Sint_Maarten.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="675" data-file-height="450">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Sint_Maarten" title="Sint Maarten">Sint Maarten</a></li>
          </ul> <p>The continental part of the Netherlands, Aruba, Curaçao, and Sint Maarten form the four constituent countries of the Kingdom. Three other territories (<a href="/wiki/Bonaire" title="Bonaire">Bonaire</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saba" title="Saba">Saba</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Sint_Eustatius" title="Sint Eustatius">Sint Eustatius</a>) are <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Netherlands" title="Caribbean Netherlands">special municipalities</a> of the continental Netherlands. </p><p>The designation "Netherlands" can refer either to the continental Netherlands or to the short name for the entire Kingdom (e.g. in international organizations). The Kingdom of the Netherlands as a whole is a member of the EU, but EU law applies only to parts within Europe. </p> </td>
        </tr>

         <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Oman"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Flag_of_Oman.svg/23px-Flag_of_Oman.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Flag_of_Oman.svg/35px-Flag_of_Oman.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/dd/Flag_of_Oman.svg/46px-Flag_of_Oman.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Oman" title="Oman">Oman</a></b>&nbsp;– Sultanate of Oman </td>

        <tr> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Pakistan"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Flag_of_Pakistan.svg/23px-Flag_of_Pakistan.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Flag_of_Pakistan.svg/35px-Flag_of_Pakistan.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Flag_of_Pakistan.svg/45px-Flag_of_Pakistan.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a></b>&nbsp;– Islamic Republic of Pakistan </td> 
         <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td> 
         <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None </td> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Pakistan is a <a href="/wiki/Federation" title="Federation">federation</a> of <a href="/wiki/Subdivisions_of_Pakistan" class="mw-redirect" title="Subdivisions of Pakistan">four provinces, 1 capital territory, and tribal regions</a>. Pakistan disputes the entire territory of <a href="/wiki/Kashmir" title="Kashmir">Kashmir</a> with <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>, and part of it with the <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">People's Republic of China</a>. It exercises control over <a href="/wiki/Pakistan-administered_Kashmir" class="mw-redirect" title="Pakistan-administered Kashmir">certain portions</a> of Kashmir, but has not officially annexed any of it,<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">[39]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">[40]</a></sup> instead regarding it as a disputed territory.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">[41]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">[42]</a></sup> The portions that it controls are divided into two territories, administered separately from Pakistan proper:<sup id="cite_ref-Kashmir_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kashmir-67">[y]</a></sup> 
          <ul>
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Flag_of_Azad_Kashmir.svg/23px-Flag_of_Azad_Kashmir.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Flag_of_Azad_Kashmir.svg/35px-Flag_of_Azad_Kashmir.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Flag_of_Azad_Kashmir.svg/45px-Flag_of_Azad_Kashmir.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="648" data-file-height="432">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Azad_Kashmir" title="Azad Kashmir">Azad Kashmir</a></li> 
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Flag_of_Gilgit-Baltistan.svg/22px-Flag_of_Gilgit-Baltistan.svg.png" decoding="async" width="22" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Flag_of_Gilgit-Baltistan.svg/33px-Flag_of_Gilgit-Baltistan.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Flag_of_Gilgit-Baltistan.svg/43px-Flag_of_Gilgit-Baltistan.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1129" data-file-height="785">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Gilgit-Baltistan" title="Gilgit-Baltistan">Gilgit Baltistan</a></li>
          </ul> <p>Azad Kashmir describes itself as a "self-governing state under Pakistani control", while Gilgit-Baltistan is described in its governance order as a group of "areas" with self-government.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">[43]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-gbtribune.files.wordpress.com_69-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gbtribune.files.wordpress.com-69">[44]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AJ&amp;KHistory_70-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AJ&amp;KHistory-70">[45]</a></sup> These territories are not usually regarded as sovereign, as they do not fulfill the criteria set out by the declarative theory of statehood (for example, their current laws do not allow them to engage independently in relations with other states). Several state functions of these territories (such as foreign affairs and defence) are performed by Pakistan.<sup id="cite_ref-gbtribune.files.wordpress.com_69-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gbtribune.files.wordpress.com-69">[44]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">[46]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">[47]</a></sup> </p> </td>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Palau"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Palau.svg/23px-Flag_of_Palau.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="14" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Palau.svg/35px-Flag_of_Palau.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/48/Flag_of_Palau.svg/46px-Flag_of_Palau.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="500">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">Palau</a></b>&nbsp;– Republic of Palau </td> 
         <td><span style="display:none">A</span> UN member state </td>

        <tr> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Palestine"></span><b><span class="datasortkey" data-sort-value="Palestine"><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/23px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/35px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/00/Flag_of_Palestine.svg/46px-Flag_of_Palestine.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/State_of_Palestine" title="State of Palestine">Palestine</a></span></b>&nbsp;– State of Palestine </td> 
         <td style="background:LightSkyBlue;"><span style="display:none">A</span> <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_observers" class="mw-redirect" title="United Nations General Assembly observers">UN observer state</a>; member of 1 <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations (not yet started)">UN specialized agency</a> </td> 
         <td style="background:LightCoral;"><a href="/w/index.php?title=International_recognition_of_the_State_of_Palestine&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="International recognition of the State of Palestine (not yet started)">Partially unrecognized</a>. <span style="display:none">B Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> </span>Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a></span> </td> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">The declared State of Palestine has received diplomatic recognition from <a href="/w/index.php?title=International_recognition_of_the_State_of_Palestine&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="International recognition of the State of Palestine (not yet started)">137</a> states.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">[48]</a></sup> The proclaimed state has no agreed territorial borders, or effective control on much of the territory that it proclaimed.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">[49]</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_National_Authority" title="Palestinian National Authority">Palestinian National Authority</a> is an interim administrative body formed as a result of the <a href="/wiki/Oslo_Accords" title="Oslo Accords">Oslo Accords</a> that exercises limited autonomous jurisdiction within the <a href="/wiki/Palestinian_territories" title="Palestinian territories">Palestinian territories</a>. In foreign relations, Palestine is represented by the <a href="/wiki/Palestine_Liberation_Organization" title="Palestine Liberation Organization">Palestine Liberation Organization</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-unnms_75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-unnms-75">[50]</a></sup> The State of Palestine is a member state of UNESCO,<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">[51]</a></sup> and an observer state in the UN. </td>
        </tr>

         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">South Sudan is a <a href="/wiki/Federation" title="Federation">federation</a> of <a href="/w/index.php?title=States_of_South_Sudan&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="States of South Sudan (not yet started)">28 states</a>. 
          <ul>
           <li>The <a href="/w/index.php?title=Abyei_Area&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Abyei Area (not yet started)">Abyei Area</a> is a zone with "special administrative status" established by the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Comprehensive_Peace_Agreement&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Comprehensive Peace Agreement (not yet started)">Comprehensive Peace Agreement</a> in 2005. It is <i>de-jure</i> a condominium of South Sudan and Sudan, but <i>de facto</i> administered by South Sudan.<sup id="cite_ref-UNISFA2017_77-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UNISFA2017-77">[52]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-AbyeiName_78-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AbyeiName-78">[53]</a></sup></li>
          </ul> </td>

         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Ukraine contains an <a href="/w/index.php?title=Territorial_autonomy&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Territorial autonomy (not yet started)">autonomous republic</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Autonomous_Republic_of_Crimea&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Autonomous Republic of Crimea (not yet started)">Crimea</a>. In 2014 Russia annexed the region along with <a href="/wiki/Sevastopol" title="Sevastopol">Sevastopol</a> turning them in one of its federal subjects as <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Crimea" title="Republic of Crimea">Republic of Crimea</a> and city of Sevastopol. </td>

         <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="United_States"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1235" data-file-height="650">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a></b>&nbsp;– United States of America </td>

         <td><span style="display:none">A</span> None </td> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">The United States is a <a href="/wiki/Federation" title="Federation">federation</a> of <a href="/wiki/Political_divisions_of_the_United_States" class="mw-redirect" title="Political divisions of the United States">50 states and 1 federal district</a> with <a href="/w/index.php?title=Shared_sovereignty&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Shared sovereignty (not yet started)">shared sovereignty</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Federal_government_of_the_United_States" title="Federal government of the United States">Federal government of the United States</a> has sovereignty over the following inhabited possessions and commonwealths: 
          <ul>
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Flag_of_American_Samoa.svg/23px-Flag_of_American_Samoa.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Flag_of_American_Samoa.svg/35px-Flag_of_American_Samoa.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/87/Flag_of_American_Samoa.svg/46px-Flag_of_American_Samoa.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="500">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/American_Samoa" title="American Samoa">American Samoa</a></li> 
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Flag_of_Guam.svg/23px-Flag_of_Guam.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Flag_of_Guam.svg/35px-Flag_of_Guam.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/Flag_of_Guam.svg/46px-Flag_of_Guam.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="820" data-file-height="440">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Guam" title="Guam">Guam</a></li> 
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/Flag_of_the_Northern_Mariana_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Northern_Mariana_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/Flag_of_the_Northern_Mariana_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Northern_Mariana_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e0/Flag_of_the_Northern_Mariana_Islands.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Northern_Mariana_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1100" data-file-height="550">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Northern_Mariana_Islands" title="Northern Mariana Islands">Northern Mariana Islands</a></li> 
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Flag_of_Puerto_Rico.svg/23px-Flag_of_Puerto_Rico.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Flag_of_Puerto_Rico.svg/35px-Flag_of_Puerto_Rico.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/28/Flag_of_Puerto_Rico.svg/45px-Flag_of_Puerto_Rico.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a></li> 
           <li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Flag_of_the_United_States_Virgin_Islands.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States_Virgin_Islands.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Flag_of_the_United_States_Virgin_Islands.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States_Virgin_Islands.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f8/Flag_of_the_United_States_Virgin_Islands.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_United_States_Virgin_Islands.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1275" data-file-height="850">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/United_States_Virgin_Islands" title="United States Virgin Islands">U.S. Virgin Islands</a></li>
          </ul> <p>It also has sovereignty over several uninhabited territories: </p> 
          <ul>
           <li><a href="/wiki/Baker_Island" title="Baker Island">Baker Island</a></li> 
           <li><a href="/wiki/Howland_Island" title="Howland Island">Howland Island</a></li> 
           <li><a href="/wiki/Jarvis_Island" title="Jarvis Island">Jarvis Island</a></li> 
           <li><a href="/wiki/Johnston_Atoll" title="Johnston Atoll">Johnston Atoll</a></li>

           <li><a href="/wiki/Midway_Atoll" title="Midway Atoll">Midway Atoll</a></li>

           <li><a href="/wiki/Wake_Island" title="Wake Island">Wake Island</a></li>
          </ul> <p>It also has sovereignty over the following incorporated territories: </p> 
          <ul>
           <li><a href="/wiki/Palmyra_Atoll" title="Palmyra Atoll">Palmyra Atoll</a></li>
          </ul> <p>Three sovereign states have become <a href="/w/index.php?title=Associated_state&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Associated state (not yet started)">associated states</a> of the United States under the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Compact_of_Free_Association&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Compact of Free Association (not yet started)">Compact of Free Association</a>: </p> 
          <ul>

         <td style="background:LightSkyBlue;"><span style="display:none">A</span> <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly_observers" class="mw-redirect" title="United Nations General Assembly observers">UN observer state</a> under the designation of "<a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Holy See</a>"; member of three <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations (not yet started)">UN specialized agencies</a> and the <a href="/wiki/International_Atomic_Energy_Agency" title="International Atomic Energy Agency">IAEA</a> </td>

         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Administered by the <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">Holy See</a>, a sovereign entity with diplomatic ties to <a href="/w/index.php?title=International_recognition_of_the_Holy_See&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="International recognition of the Holy See (not yet started)">183&nbsp;states</a> – 180 UN member states, one UN observer state (Palestine), the Cook Islands and the Republic of China (Taiwan).<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">[54]</a></sup> The Holy See is a member of the <a href="/wiki/International_Atomic_Energy_Agency" title="International Atomic Energy Agency">IAEA</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=International_Telecommunication_Union&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="International Telecommunication Union (not yet started)">ITU</a>, <a href="/w/index.php?title=Universal_Postal_Union&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Universal Postal Union (not yet started)">UPU</a>, and <a href="/w/index.php?title=World_Intellectual_Property_Organization&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="World Intellectual Property Organization (not yet started)">WIPO</a> and a permanent observer of the UN (in the category of "Non-member State")<sup id="cite_ref-unnms_75-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-unnms-75">[50]</a></sup> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Foreign_relations_of_the_Holy_See&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Foreign relations of the Holy See (not yet started)">multiple other UN System organizations</a>. The Vatican City is governed by officials appointed by the <a href="/wiki/Pope" title="Pope">Pope</a>, who is the Bishop of the Diocese of Rome and <i><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ex_officio&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ex officio (not yet started)">ex officio</a></i> sovereign of Vatican City. </td>

         <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Kosovo"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Flag_of_Kosovo.svg/21px-Flag_of_Kosovo.svg.png" decoding="async" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Flag_of_Kosovo.svg/32px-Flag_of_Kosovo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1f/Flag_of_Kosovo.svg/42px-Flag_of_Kosovo.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="840" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a></b>&nbsp;– Republic of Kosovo </td> 
         <td style="background:lightgreen;"><span style="display:none">D</span> Member of two <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations (not yet started)">UN specialized agencies</a> </td> 
         <td style="background:LightCoral;"><span style="display:none">B Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a> </span>Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a></span> </td> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">Pursuant to <a href="/w/index.php?title=United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_1244&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 1244 (not yet started)">United Nations Security Council Resolution 1244</a>, Kosovo was placed under the administration of the <a href="/w/index.php?title=United_Nations_Interim_Administration_Mission_in_Kosovo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="United Nations Interim Administration Mission in Kosovo (not yet started)">United Nations Interim Administration Mission in Kosovo</a> in 1999.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">[62]</a></sup> Kosovo <a href="/wiki/2008_Kosovo_declaration_of_independence" title="2008 Kosovo declaration of independence">declared independence in 2008</a>, and it has <a href="/w/index.php?title=International_recognition_of_Kosovo&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="International recognition of Kosovo (not yet started)">received diplomatic recognition from&nbsp;113&nbsp;UN member states</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" title="Republic of China">Republic of China</a>. Serbia continues to maintain its sovereignty claim over Kosovo. Other UN member states and non UN member states continue to recognise Serbian sovereignty or have taken no position on the question. Kosovo is a member of the <a href="/wiki/International_Monetary_Fund" title="International Monetary Fund">International Monetary Fund</a> and the <a href="/wiki/World_Bank_Group" title="World Bank Group">World Bank Group</a>. The Republic of Kosovo has de facto control over most of the territory, with limited control in <a href="/wiki/North_Kosovo" title="North Kosovo">North Kosovo</a>. </td>
        </tr>

        <tr> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;"><span id="Taiwan"></span><b><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_Republic_of_China.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600">&nbsp;</span><a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a></b>&nbsp;– Republic of China<sup id="cite_ref-ChinaTaiwan_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ChinaTaiwan-21">[l]</a></sup> </td> 
         <td style="background:Orchid;"><span style="display:none">D</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=China_and_the_United_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="China and the United Nations (not yet started)">Former UN member</a> (as Republic of China, 1945–1971)<br>Observer in one <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations (not yet started)">UN specialized agency</a> under the name "<a href="/wiki/Chinese_Taipei" class="mw-redirect" title="Chinese Taipei">Chinese Taipei</a>" </td> 
         <td style="background:LightCoral;"><span style="display:none">B Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> </span>Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a></span> </td> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">A state competing (nominally) for recognition with the <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">People's Republic of China</a> (PRC) as the government of China since 1949. The Republic of China (ROC) controls the island of <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a> and associated islands, Quemoy, Matsu, the Pratas and parts of the <a href="/wiki/Spratly_Islands" title="Spratly Islands">Spratly Islands</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-Spratly_97-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Spratly-97">[aa]</a></sup> and has not renounced claims over its annexed territories on the <a href="/wiki/Mainland_China" title="Mainland China">mainland</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">[71]</a></sup> The ROC is recognised by <a href="/w/index.php?title=International_recognition_of_the_Republic_of_China&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="International recognition of the Republic of China (not yet started)">16</a> UN member states and the Holy See as of 21 August 2018. All these states do not recognise the PRC either. Additionally, one UN member (<a href="/wiki/Bhutan" title="Bhutan">Bhutan</a>) has <a href="/w/index.php?title=Foreign_relations_of_Taiwan&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Foreign relations of Taiwan (not yet started)">refrained from recognising</a> either the ROC or the PRC. <p>The territory of the ROC is claimed in whole by the PRC.<sup id="cite_ref-TAI2_22-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TAI2-22">[m]</a></sup> The ROC <a href="/w/index.php?title=Foreign_relations_of_Taiwan&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Foreign relations of Taiwan (not yet started)">participates in international organizations</a> under a variety of pseudonyms, most commonly "<a href="/wiki/Chinese_Taipei" class="mw-redirect" title="Chinese Taipei">Chinese Taipei</a>" and in the <a href="/wiki/World_Trade_Organization" title="World Trade Organization">WTO</a> it has full membership. The ROC was a founding member of the UN and enjoyed membership from 1945 to 1971, with veto power in the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">UN Security Council</a>. See <a href="/w/index.php?title=China_and_the_United_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="China and the United Nations (not yet started)">China and the United Nations</a>. </p> </td>
        </tr>

         <td style="background:LemonChiffon;"><span style="display:none">D</span> No membership </td> 
         <td style="background:LightCoral;"><span style="display:none">B Claimed by <a href="#Georgia">Georgia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_North">North Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Serbia">Serbia</a> Claimed by <a href="#Somalia">Somalia</a> Claimed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a> Claimed by <a href="#Korea_South">South Korea</a> Claimed by <a href="#Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a> Claimed by the <a href="#Cyprus">Republic of Cyprus</a> Disputed by <a href="#Israel">Israel</a> Claimed by <a href="#Mauritius">Mauritius</a> Claimed by <a href="#Morocco">Morocco</a> </span>Claimed by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a><span style="display:none"> Claimed by <a href="#Mali">Mali</a> Claimed by <a href="#Spain">Spain</a></span> </td> 
         <td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left;font-size:90%;">A de facto independent state,<sup id="cite_ref-montevideo_82-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-montevideo-82">[56]</a></sup> <a href="/w/index.php?title=Foreign_relations_of_Transnistria&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Foreign relations of Transnistria (not yet started)">recognised only by</a> Abkhazia, Artsakh and South Ossetia.<sup id="cite_ref-ASOTREC_81-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ASOTREC-81">[55]</a></sup> Claimed in whole by <a href="#Moldova">Moldova</a> as the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Transnistria_autonomous_territorial_unit_with_special_legal_status&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Transnistria autonomous territorial unit with special legal status (not yet started)">Transnistria autonomous territorial unit</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">[72]</a></sup> </td>
        </tr>

         <li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-1">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text">This column indicates whether or not a state is a member of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a>. It also indicates which non-member states participate in the <a href="/w/index.php?title=United_Nations_System&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="United Nations System (not yet started)">United Nations System</a> through membership in the <a href="/wiki/International_Atomic_Energy_Agency" title="International Atomic Energy Agency">International Atomic Energy Agency</a> or one of the <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_specialized_agencies_of_the_United_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="List of specialized agencies of the United Nations (not yet started)">specialized agencies of the United Nations</a>. All United Nations members belong to at least one specialized agency and are parties to the statute of the <a href="/wiki/International_Court_of_Justice" title="International Court of Justice">International Court of Justice</a>.</span> </li>

         <li id="cite_note-UNASUL-10"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">↑ <sup><a href="#cite_ref-UNASUL_10-0">8.00</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-UNASUL_10-1">8.01</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-UNASUL_10-2">8.02</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-UNASUL_10-3">8.03</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-UNASUL_10-4">8.04</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-UNASUL_10-5">8.05</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-UNASUL_10-6">8.06</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-UNASUL_10-7">8.07</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-UNASUL_10-8">8.08</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-UNASUL_10-9">8.09</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-UNASUL_10-10">8.10</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-UNASUL_10-11">8.11</a></sup></span> <span class="reference-text">The member states of the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Union_of_South_American_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Union of South American Nations (not yet started)">Union of South American Nations</a> have transferred part of their sovereignty in the form of legislative, executive, and judicial powers to the institutions of the UNASUL, which is an example of <a href="/w/index.php?title=Supranational_union&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Supranational union (not yet started)">supranational union</a>.          <li id="cite_note-ChinaTaiwan-21"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">↑ <sup><a href="#cite_ref-ChinaTaiwan_21-0">12.0</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-ChinaTaiwan_21-1">12.1</a></sup></span> <span class="reference-text">The <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">People's Republic of China</a> (PRC) is commonly referred to as "China", while the <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Republic of China</a> (ROC) is commonly referred to as "Taiwan". The ROC is also occasionally known diplomatically as <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Taipei" class="mw-redirect" title="Chinese Taipei">Chinese Taipei</a>, along with <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Taipei#Other_alternative_references_to_the_Republic_of_China" class="mw-redirect" title="Chinese Taipei">other names</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-TAI2-22"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">↑ <sup><a href="#cite_ref-TAI2_22-0">13.0</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-TAI2_22-1">13.1</a></sup></span> <span class="reference-text">In 1949, the Republic of China government led by the <a href="/wiki/Kuomintang" title="Kuomintang">Kuomintang</a> (KMT) lost the <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Civil_War" title="Chinese Civil War">Chinese Civil War</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Communist_Party_of_China" title="Communist Party of China">Communist Party of China</a> (CPC) and set up a provisional capital in <a href="/wiki/Taipei" title="Taipei">Taipei</a>. The CPC established the PRC. As such, the <a href="/wiki/Political_status_of_Taiwan" title="Political status of Taiwan">political status of the ROC and legal status of Taiwan</a> (alongside the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Free_area_of_the_Republic_of_China&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Free area of the Republic of China (not yet started)">territories</a> under ROC jurisdiction) are in dispute. In 1971, the United Nations gave the <a href="/w/index.php?title=China_and_the_United_Nations&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="China and the United Nations (not yet started)">China seat</a> to the PRC and the ROC withdrew from the UN. Most states recognise the PRC to be the <a href="/w/index.php?title=One-China_policy&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="One-China policy (not yet started)">sole legitimate representative</a> of all China, and the UN classifies Taiwan as "<a href="/wiki/Taiwan_Province,_People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="Taiwan Province, People's Republic of China">Taiwan, Province of China</a>". The ROC has de facto relations with most sovereign states. A significant political movement within Taiwan advocates <a href="/w/index.php?title=Taiwan_independence_movement&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Taiwan independence movement (not yet started)">Taiwan independence</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-23"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-23">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text">See also <a href="/w/index.php?title=Dates_of_establishment_of_diplomatic_relations_with_the_People%27s_Republic_of_China&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Dates of establishment of diplomatic relations with the People's Republic of China (not yet started)">Dates of establishment of diplomatic relations with the People's Republic of China</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Foreign_relations_of_China&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Foreign relations of China (not yet started)">Foreign relations of China</a>.</span> </li>

         <li id="cite_note-30"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-30">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text">A simpler official short name has been encouraged by the Czech government, "<i>Czechia</i>". By 2017, this variant remains uncommon. Nevertheless, this term has been adopted by several companies and organisations, including Google Maps, instead of the term "<i>Czech Republic</i>". See <a href="/w/index.php?title=Name_of_the_Czech_Republic&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Name of the Czech Republic (not yet started)">Name of the Czech Republic</a></span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-33"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-33">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text">The government of East Timor uses "Timor-Leste" as the English translation.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-36"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-36">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text"><a href="/wiki/%C3%85land_Islands" title="Åland Islands">Åland</a> was demilitarised by the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Treaty_of_Paris_(1856)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Treaty of Paris (1856) (not yet started)">Treaty of Paris</a> in 1856, which was later affirmed by the <a href="/wiki/League_of_Nations" title="League of Nations">League of Nations</a> in 1921, and in a somewhat different context reaffirmed in the treaty on Finland's admission to the European Union in 1995.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-39"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-39">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text">Also known as Guinea-Conakry.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-Republic-43"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-Republic_43-0">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text">While sometimes referred to as the "<b>Republic of Iceland</b>"<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">[19]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">[20]</a></sup> and sometimes its counterpart <i>Lýðveldið Ísland</i> in Icelandic, the official name of the country is simply Iceland.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">[21]</a></sup> One example of the former is the name of the <a href="/w/index.php?title=Constitution_of_Iceland&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Constitution of Iceland (not yet started)">Constitution of Iceland</a>, which in Icelandic is <i>Stjórnarskrá lýðveldisins Íslands</i> and literally means "the Constitution of the republic of Iceland", but note that "republic" is not capitalized. The official title of the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Iceland" title="President of Iceland">President of Iceland</a> (<i>Forseti Íslands</i>) does also not include the word republic as in some other republics. See <a href="/w/index.php?title=Names_for_Iceland&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Names for Iceland (not yet started)">Names for Iceland</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-koreas-55"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">↑ <sup><a href="#cite_ref-koreas_55-0">23.0</a></sup> <sup><a href="#cite_ref-koreas_55-1">23.1</a></sup></span> <span class="reference-text">Both North Korea and South Korea claim to be the sole legitimate government of <a href="/wiki/Korea" title="Korea">Korea</a>. See also <a href="/w/index.php?title=Foreign_relations_of_North_Korea&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Foreign relations of North Korea (not yet started)">Foreign relations of North Korea</a> and <a href="/w/index.php?title=Foreign_relations_of_South_Korea&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Foreign relations of South Korea (not yet started)">Foreign relations of South Korea</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">[32]</a></sup></span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-58"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-58">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text">The government changed the state's official name in English from "Union of Myanmar" to "Republic of the Union of Myanmar" in October 2010.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">[34]</a></sup></span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-Kashmir-67"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-Kashmir_67-0">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text">Sovereignty over <a href="/wiki/Kashmir" title="Kashmir">Kashmir</a> is disputed between <a href="#India">India</a> and <a href="#Pakistan">Pakistan</a>; smaller parts are disputed by the <a href="#China">People's Republic of China</a> and the <a href="#Taiwan">Republic of China</a>. Kashmir is divided between India, Pakistan and the PRC. See the <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_territorial_disputes&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="List of territorial disputes (not yet started)">List of territorial disputes</a>.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-79"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-79">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text">Formerly known as <a href="/wiki/Dominion_of_Ceylon" class="mw-redirect" title="Dominion of Ceylon">Ceylon</a> until 1972.</span> </li> 
         <li id="cite_note-Spratly-97"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><a href="#cite_ref-Spratly_97-0">↑</a></span> <span class="reference-text">The sovereignty over the <a href="/wiki/Spratly_Islands" title="Spratly Islands">Spratly Islands</a> is disputed by <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>, <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>, <a href="#Vietnam">Vietnam</a>, and in part by <a href="#Brunei">Brunei</a>, <a href="#Malaysia">Malaysia</a>, and the <a href="#Philippines">Philippines</a>. Except for Brunei, each of these countries occupies part of the islands (see <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_territorial_disputes&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="List of territorial disputes (not yet started)">List of territorial disputes</a>).</span> </li> 
        </ol>
       </div>
      </div> <!--
